Free Talk

World Snippets

— Hai Ke

Reading Materials and Entertainment in British Prisons

In most people's minds, criminals in prison, if they don't like to read, so be it. But if they do like to read, they must love detective novels because detective novels describe bandits and petty thieves, which can give them some criminal tricks that will be very useful after they are released from prison. However, according to reports from prison officials across England, the most popular reading material among criminals is Shakespeare and Bernard Shaw's plays. It's hard to know what that means. They love reading plays even more than novels, and the works of these two masters are profound and difficult to understand. In addition, there is the famous play "Abraham Lincoln," which tells the story of the life of American President Lincoln, and it is often found in prison cells. This shows that the conscience of criminals has not been extinguished, and they also admire great figures in the world. Regarding entertainment, Maidstone Prison is equipped with radio, where inmates can listen to music and songs, as well as various speeches on ethics and science. Bediford Prison has a dance class that is taught once a week, and Birmingham Prison even has sports field facilities, with all kinds of sports equipment available. This is what criminals are most satisfied with.

Naughty Boy's Prank

— Yi

In recent months, there have been reports of ginkgo trees spontaneously combusting. People who love gossip have deliberately mystified the situation, spreading all kinds of bizarre and absurd stories. Superstitious people follow suit, often causing a sensation far and wide. According to what I have heard, the spontaneous combustion of a ginkgo tree in front of an ancient temple on Datong Bridge in Pengzhen, Kunshan, is particularly valued by the general public. Although several months have passed, the rumors have not subsided. This journal has also recorded similar events, but I don't remember whether it was the one that occurred in Kunshan. When the tree spontaneously combusted, nearby residents went to rescue it, but to no avail. It was also heard that someone shouted that the temple god had ascended to heaven and the ginkgo tree was emitting smoke. It is unknown who said this. The crowd became suspicious and fearful, believing it to be a divine phenomenon. As a result, it spontaneously combusted for three days and three nights, turning into a charred tree. Again, it is unknown who spread rumors, claiming that the ginkgo tree fruit had become a god, and that praying to it could cure any incurable disease. Superstitious believers believed it and went to pray. Some people also said that the tree roots and the vegetation around them were all elixirs, which could be taken home and stored for miraculous effects in treating diseases. As a result, within a few days, people took everything away. What was originally rotten and foul was transformed into something miraculous. Before long, the story spread to hundreds of miles away. People from neighboring counties also rushed to the scene, with vehicles and footprints lining the road. The authorities did not stop it, allowing the rumors to mislead the public and collecting incense money to rebuild the temple. To this day, people from all directions are still flocking to the site, especially on the first and fifteenth days of the lunar month. Initially, it was not limited to ignorant villagers; even the educated class was deceived by it. At its peak, the incense and donation money could reach four to five hundred gold pieces per month. This ancient temple, which was once deserted, will soon be transformed into a magnificent and solemn monastery. In fact, the reason for the tree's spontaneous combustion was a prank by a naughty boy. Because the tree was old, the trunk was hollow, and there was a hole at the root. Before the spontaneous combustion, the naughty boy was playing under the tree and stuffed straw into the hole and set it on fire, resulting in this outcome. The words "the temple god ascended to heaven and the ginkgo tree emitted smoke" were also shouted by the naughty boy. Moreover, ginkgo trees are prone to being struck by lightning and spontaneously combusting. Therefore, it is not surprising that they are often struck by lightning, even if it is not a prank by a naughty boy. Now, the superstitious talk in that area has deeply penetrated people's hearts. Even though the cause has been revealed, people refuse to believe it and firmly believe that the tree is still divine. This is regrettable.

Shanghai's Enticing Trap

— Chi Fo

The "Axe Gang" is a branch of the Triads and the Green Gang. In areas such as Hongkou in Shanghai, assassinations and armed fights often occur, using axes as weapons. We often hear about it and are not surprised. Recently, cases of enticing traps have been discovered in Shanghai. Their nature is very similar to the old "fairy jump" and "sliding door" schemes, but their methods are even more ruthless. They often use the law as a shield for extortion. Those who fall into their trap have no choice but to submit. Even with a hundred mouths, they cannot defend themselves. They can only eagerly pay up and fill their insatiable desires, lamenting that they have fallen into a trap. People therefore call them the "Female Axe Gang." My old friend Mr. W, who is well-known in the business world, occasionally indulges in seeking pleasure among flowers and willows after managing his business affairs. He is not a libertine. One day, while watching a movie in a large cinema, when the lights dimmed, a beautiful woman gracefully came and sat next to Mr. W. Her oriole-like voice occasionally teased Mr. W with jokes. Who is without feelings? Who can resist this? After frequent conversations, they exchanged backgrounds. Their eyes conveyed affection, and their souls were given to each other. After the play, they went to a restaurant together. The woman said that she was from Wu, eighteen years old, and her brother was responsible for the cashier's duties at a certain bank. She was currently living with her mother in a certain neighborhood in western Shanghai. In the depths of the green shade, a corner of a building was her home. She hoped that Mr. W would visit when he had time. Mr. W was very happy, thinking that he had met Yunying on the Blue Bridge, and that Peach Blossom Spring was not far away and the fisherman could inquire about it. From then on, they visited each other frequently and discussed marriage. Mr. W falsely claimed that he was unmarried and willing to make a lifelong commitment. On the night of their engagement, the woman's brother and mother also participated, and there were no objections at first. Before two months had passed, the woman suddenly hired a lawyer to sue Mr. W for bigamy in court. Her brother also threatened him with the crime of raping a girl under the age of twenty. The woman was like a different person. Not only was Mr. W a stranger, but she also regarded him as a deep-seated enemy. At first, Mr. W was still in a daze, thinking that the sea of hatred was hard to fill, the waves of love were rough, and the joyous face could be picked up again. Later, the threats became more and more intense, and there was clearly no emotion to speak of. However, due to his own reputation and status, he had no choice but to have a mediator like Lu Lian come forward to mediate, and the matter was settled with 5,000 gold pieces. Later, someone who knew about the matter sighed and said that this was the trick of the "Female Axe Gang." Their organization is quite perfect, with more than a thousand members in Shanghai. It is said that the profits are many times greater than opening a Korean geisha house. Their goal is to focus on prominent figures, wealthy merchants, and high-ranking officials in Shanghai, as their concerns about face make them easy to blackmail.

Japan's Match Business in China

— Wan Cheng

Japan's economic aggression, even with the match industry alone, is alarming enough. The Pootung Japanese Zuisan Match Factory is entirely manufactured by machines, with only four hundred workers. The Dachunghua Match Company Rongchang Factory has one thousand three or four hundred workers. According to people in the match industry, the products of the two match factories are on par. Also, the matches produced by the "Mingguang Company" on the market are printed with "Made in Sweden," but are actually produced by the Japanese Zuisan Factory. In the midst of the Sino-Japanese economic severance, this is something we should be aware of. I hope my compatriots will pay attention to it.

Jumbled Fan Talk

— Yan Zi

Shanghai's painting exhibitions can be considered to be at their peak. During this sweltering summer heat, fan painting exhibitions can also rise in popularity. Shen Junyouren of Huzhou excels at writing hairpin-style small regular script. He can write a seven-character Tang poem on a grain of millet. Those who see it marvel at his superb skills. Shen has close friendships with people in the art world. He recently launched a fan painting exhibition at the New World's third floor. For a time, famous painters such as Wang Zhongshan, Xiong Songquan, Zhang Huian, Yao Hongzhao, Kong Xiaoyu, Ye Weishen, Gao Shangzhi, Wang Yunsheng, Xu Xiaocun, and Yin Zixiang were all recruited. The fan surfaces are all original designs, custom-made to order, much like the open-pit mining method in porcelain. Gold backgrounds are used for writing, and white backgrounds are used for painting extremely detailed landscapes, figures, flowers, birds, and animals, all of which are exquisitely crafted. It is a rare sight to behold. Entering the room, one immediately feels that the four walls are full of treasures, and one's eyes cannot take it all in. I love the most exquisite fan surfaces, such as the ink plum blossoms painted by Li Fangyuan. In the middle, there is a white background in the style of a book scroll, painted with detailed landscapes by Zhang Huian, Xu Xiaocun, and others. With every inch a thousand miles, the brushstrokes are full of remaining charm. Kong Xiaoyu's antique flower arrangements are antique and elegant, even more exquisite. Wang Yunsheng's animals are full of life and seem to leap to life. In the branches and trunks of the plum blossoms, Shen Jun writes hundreds of plum blossom poems in small regular script, with a charming style, like a seventeen or eighteen year old girl, making people love them endlessly. They can be regarded as doubly exquisite.

Record of the Gu Lin Jing She

— Qiu Kefu

Ancient countries must read ancient books. Ancient books are all in ancient language, which is different from modern language. Therefore, one must be proficient in the art of translation in order to translate ancient language into modern language. However, some errors in translation have persisted for a long time, uncorrected for two thousand years. The Qing scholars arose, questioning every word, character, sound, and meaning. They extensively examined various translations to find the true meaning of the ancient language. Once found, they did not immediately believe it. They also sought other evidence to support it. Only when all the evidence was the same, without any discrepancies, did they believe it to be true. Therefore, once a meaning is clarified, all doubts cease. Even if the translator were to rise from the underworld, he would have to sigh in admiration. The Qing scholars' meticulous research on language was like this. My friend Jun Zhonghu has long been fond of this learning and has made many discoveries. Recently, he has also analyzed and extracted the Shuowen Jiezi, the Great and Small Xu versions, and the Qing scholars' special books on philology, or those scattered in other books, arranging them by character to create a book called Gu Lin, hoping to reduce the daily effort of studying ancient texts and benefit learning for the ages. After the book was completed, he named his residence Gu Lin Jing She and asked me to write a record for it. The Jing She has a collection of 150,000 volumes, which is Zhonghu's place for writing books. He holds tea parties there whenever there is a constellation. This has been going on for ten years. The Jing She has changed its location several times, but the tea parties remain the same. On the appointed day, as the sun sets, the guests all arrive. The wind, rain, cold, and heat do not deter them. However, only Mr. Wu Zhihui has often helped the host to determine the format, which has been of great help to Gu Lin.

Correction: In the article "Record of What I Saw at the Jiangyin Garden Hotel" published in this column on the 23rd, a character "屠" (屠) was missing after the character "龍" (龍) in the fifteenth line. Also, in the article "The Alarming Search for Commercial Information by the Japanese in Shanghai" published on the 26th, the first character "我" (I) was a mistake for "日" (日).

Random Talk About the Lives of American Women (III)

— Ji

▲ Marriage: American women are not too demanding in their conditions for marriage. For example, a high school graduate is willing to marry a high school student, and a college graduate is willing to marry a college student. There are no demands to marry someone of a higher level. This is more accommodating than women in our country. The conditions they consider important are a strong physique, pure character, a spirit of service, and they don't care about the other person's wealth. They believe that people with wealth often have habits of laziness, arrogance, and extravagance. They only enjoy pleasure and cannot endure hardship. Moreover, they have their own jobs and can be economically independent, so they don't need to rely on their husbands for support. This detached view is very admirable. The choice of marriage is completely free. It starts with friendship and goes through a long period of careful consideration of each other. Only after a deep understanding and with the permission of their parents do they get engaged. There are also some couples who don't reveal their relationship beforehand. On the day of the engagement, they invite relatives and friends and announce the process of their engagement at a tea party or banquet. In the past, the marriage age in America was between twenty-five and thirty-five for men and between twenty-three and twenty-eight for women. Now it has been brought forward. However, early marriages are very rare. Because they haven't graduated from college and can't be economically independent, they absolutely cannot get married before the legal age of twenty. Their marriage ceremonies are mostly very simple. Religious people follow church rituals and ask a pastor to officiate the wedding. Non-religious people ask a respected person in the community or a local official to officiate the wedding. Before the wedding, the most important thing is to apply to the government for a marriage certificate. If the authorities do not approve and do not give the certificate, it cannot be legally established and will not be protected by law. In recent years, the number of divorce cases in America has been alarming. Among the forty-eight states in the country, the laws are different. In some states, due to religious reasons, divorce is absolutely not allowed by law. But in Reno, Nevada, divorce is absolutely possible. Some people say that the Reno city government's annual tax revenue is very small and insufficient to cover expenses, so this is a way to increase revenue. This seems to be a strategy to absorb the economy. Therefore, Americans divorcing have discovered two very strange phenomena. For example, if one party of a couple is unwilling to fulfill the conditions of the court's judgment and creates obstacles, there are two ways to go. Wealthy people go to France in the name of traveling to carry out the divorce (because the procedures in France are simple) and fulfill their wishes. People who are not economically well-off go to Reno to divorce to save money. It is said that the once deserted city of Reno has become lively due to the large number of people from various states divorcing. The income of the city government has also increased unexpectedly. As for single people, there are also quite a few. Some men are single due to unemployment and economic pressure, while a few women with millions of dollars are also single. However, the number of women who are economically independent and not feeling difficult in making a living is ultimately small. The so-called single is just a very small number.

Rotary Club Novel

Woman Woman (III)

— Yao Su Feng

Mr. Lu's visit seemed to be within Miss Ding's expectations. Because when Qiu Zi was serving them tea, she heard Miss Ding say, "Why did you only come today?"

Since arriving at the Ding's house, it was the first time that Qiu Zi saw Miss Ding meet her own friends. In a curious mood, she had already forgotten that she should no longer stay in this reception room. Until Miss Ding had no choice but to order her, "You go out! Maybe someone else will come, or there will be a phone call, refuse them all for me!"

Qiu Zi smiled in agreement and slowly retreated, but when she closed the door, she secretly saw Miss Ding already sitting down, sitting side by side with that Mr. Lu on a double sofa.

In the reception room, there was only a quiet atmosphere. Miss Ding seemed to have nothing to say, and Mr. Lu could only talk casually, from the continuous heavy rain to the dwindling of their interest in traveling. Miss Ding then said, "When the weather clears up, I really want to go to another city for a good trip."

"Have you not gone out to play since you had your holiday?" Mr. Lu asked.

"I've never gone out to play. Although Li Wenyao has written several letters, I've never paid attention to him. Yesterday he even called to ask me to play mini golf, but I declined on the pretext of being sick," Miss Ding said seemingly sincerely.

"Li Wenyao is really pitiful. He doesn't know his own boredom. His history of being dumped is known to everyone at school. He also vaguely published a novel in the school journal, but people laughed at him for having other intentions, and said that his novel was a disguised marriage advertisement!"

"I don't care about these things! However, playing with someone who has different interests always feels uninteresting. So, I welcome your visit," Miss Ding said, her eyes looking directly at Mr. Lu's face.

Mr. Lu suddenly stood up and walked slowly over, but then quickly walked back. He said to Miss Ding in an extremely gentle voice, "I really don't know what to use to repay you for your kindness to me."

Miss Ding smiled slightly. But she didn't say a word. This was clearly a time when a march was being played rapidly on Mr. Lu's leaping heartstrings.

"I have prepared a memorable thing, maybe you can accept me. It's just... maybe you can reject me! I think I will have the best of luck tomorrow," Mr. Lu said very gently.

But Miss Ding still only smiled slightly. Mr. Lu naturally already felt that there was a very successful hope. At this time, the night had already deeply enveloped the earth, and Mr. Lu then bid farewell and left. Miss Ding then opened her mouth and said a word, "Tomorrow, I'll be waiting for you!"

Money Market Gradually Tightening

▲Market Overview: Since late spring and early summer, the financial industry has experienced a prolonged period of sluggishness in the money market and foreign exchange, especially the silent state of the money market. Due to the impact of Japanese goods and the settlement of foreign goods, short-term financing is becoming increasingly tight. According to general speculation, the market may experience an emergency situation after the end of this month.

▲Interbank Lending Rates: (Foreign Exchange) The interbank lending rate in the morning market was 7 yuan, 2 fen, 5 li, 3 hao, and 7 hu, 5 si. The afternoon market was 7 yuan, 2 fen, and 5.5 li. The result was only 0.25 hao lower than the afternoon market of the previous day, and the situation was mostly calm. (Silver Lending) The morning market was 8 fen, and the afternoon market was 1 qian. The situation was apparently loose but actually tight, so the blended rate with added funds was still at 1 qian and 3 or 4 fen. However, all parties felt short of funds. Fortunately, the lending rate was unique and there were no major changes.

▲Subsidiary Coin Market: Jiangnan small dollars were 6 qian and 5 fen in both the morning and afternoon markets, slightly better than the previous day's afternoon market by 0.25 hao. The trading volume was 6,000 jiao in the morning market and 3,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Guangdong small dollars were 6 qian, 4 fen, and 3 li in the morning market, and 6 qian, 4 fen, 3 li, 1 hao, and 2 hu in the afternoon market. The trading volume was 125,000 jiao in the morning market and 70,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Copper coins increased by 2,000 wen to 380,000 wen, with a trading volume of over 29,000 strings.

▲Silver and Foreign Exchange Inflow and Outflow: (Silver) Yesterday, the bank's receipts and disbursements were unremarkable, with only some pledge transactions. Chinese merchants' receipts and disbursements totaled 2.45 million, foreign merchants 1.78 million, various goods, foreign exchange taxes, and miscellaneous receipts and disbursements totaled 1.01 million, pledge transactions amounted to 1.45 million, special receipts and disbursements were over 1 million, and warehouse receipts were 1.1 million. Japanese banks' receipts and disbursements of various items totaled over 4.3 million, and warehouse withdrawals were 300,000. Money shops and silver brokers' receipts and disbursements totaled over 47.7 million, blended funds totaled over 4.33 million, remittances from various sources totaled over 900,000, and cash disbursements were several tens of thousands. (Foreign Exchange) The foreign exchange clearing volume was 1.278 million in the morning market, and banknotes were only traded off-market for 150,000. In the afternoon market, the clearing volume was 915,000, banknotes were 20,000, and off-market trading was 105,000. Bank transactions were 650,000 in the morning market and 550,000 in the afternoon market. Transactions between foreign exchange accounts of various banks totaled over 1.5 million, and banknotes recovered and issued were over 1.89 million. Money shops and foreign brokers' receipts and disbursements totaled over 5.6 million, foreign exchange blended funds totaled over 1.9 million, interbank lending of foreign exchange totaled over 1.6 million, small money shops' transactions were 700,000 to 800,000, and customer remittances remained unheard of.

Securities: Stock Exchange Closed Today

▲Handling July Futures Delivery and Settlement

▲Only August Futures Opened Yesterday, Prices Continued to Weaken

Yesterday, the market conditions for various bonds and securities in the local stock market showed scarce spot transactions. In the futures market, the July contract was halted in preparation for delivery, while the September contract had not yet opened. The August contract saw some trading, but due to the proximity of delivery, major players were cautious and the market was quiet. The bond market was also very dull. Market sentiment was weak, buying interest was quite low, and prices did not fluctuate significantly. Overall, the results were consistently lower than the previous day. For example, the 20 Customs bonds for August each fell by over 1 yuan, the Disbandment 29 Customs bonds also fell slightly by 0.8 or 0.9 jiao, and the Consolidated Tax bonds continued to fall by 2.2 yuan due to some selling. The stock exchange is closed today to handle the July futures delivery and settlement, and tomorrow for delivery, so the market is closed for trading. The trading volume for futures yesterday was only 6.7 million, of which the 20-year Consolidated Tax bonds accounted for 870,000, the lowest since the opening. Spot transactions totaled 28,000 yuan.

Yarn and Cotton: Yarn Market Under Heavy Pressure

The yarn market is slightly weak, and the trend is becoming increasingly softer. The overseas cotton yarn situation is consistently trending downward, silver prices are rising, and the gold market is falling, leading to increased market fatigue. Moreover, heavy pressure from major players is making it difficult to boost the market. However, current yarn sales are still doing well. Northern merchants are still actively looking for deals, and Cantonese merchants' imports are also smooth. However, the general public and retail investors are still nervous about the boycott movement, and their bullish sentiment is still present. Rongxinghao is also purchasing, making future prospects still difficult to predict.

▲Nearby Futures Remain Strong: The exchange's opening for cotton futures saw declines of 2, 3, 4, and 5 qian due to weak US cotton and a weak market. In the afternoon, there were further declines of 3, 4, and 5 qian. However, the current month remained strong. The trading volume was 34,750 bales. Sales included 600 bales from Jifeng, 650 bales from Gongtai, 850 bales from Rongxing, 1,550 bales from Xincheng, 900 bales from Tongyu, and 1,250 bales from Hengde. Purchases included 1,450 bales from Dafu, 2,450 bales from Rongxing, 750 bales from Gengfeng, and 850 bales from Ruida. The closing prices for cotton futures are recorded below.

Cotton Market Extremely Weak

▲Weather Clears Up...Sellers Begin to Emerge

▲Gold Prices Fall...Market Shakes

US cotton shows no signs of improvement. The weather in the local area has cleared up, leading to market sentiment loosening. There are fewer buyers, and the market is shaking greatly. The downward trend is quite strong. Furthermore, many local merchants are inclined to sell, so any adverse conditions lead to more violent reactions. However, merchants from Hubei are purchasing slightly. According to various reports, cotton fields have suffered considerable damage. However, the overseas cotton market is weak, silver prices are rising, and gold prices are weak, further emboldening the short sellers.

▲Hubei Cotton Drops 6 Qian: The exchange's opening for Hubei cotton futures saw declines of 3 and 4 qian for all months due to the weather clearing up and flat external cotton prices. In the afternoon, there was another decline of 2.5 qian. The trading volume was 75,100 dan. Sales included 2,800 dan from Taixing, 3,100 dan from Jifeng, 3,500 dan from Hengde, and 4,600 dan from Xinheng. Purchases included 2,800 dan from Dafu, 4,300 dan from Guangfeng, 4,500 dan from Shenchang, 2,800 dan from Rongxing, and 2,100 dan from Changfeng. Grains: Rice Market Set for Price Increase

▲Xinzha: Yesterday, the weather cleared up, and the sources from the West Road were around the 30th. The situation was completely unrecoverable. Changxi thick glutinous rice was bid up tightly in the morning, but it weakened by noon, and prices fell back by as much as 5 jiao. However, the transaction volume was extremely stagnant. Due to the continuous sharp rise in thin rice, there will inevitably be a surge in arrivals from the rear, and the overall market has not seen any upward movement. Arrivals of Luyang pointed rice are not abundant, and the appetite is also sluggish. Glutinous rice sales are extremely strong, and the situation is stable. There is no Baopu pointed rice available on the market.

▲South Market: There are not many ships arriving from various routes, and retail sales in urban and rural shops are becoming increasingly sluggish. Suzhou white glutinous rice is tightly priced, and the appetite for Pingwang, Lili, and Beitan goods is limited, with no price fluctuations. There are only two loads of thin rice on the market, and the overall market lacks goods. The rest is Songjiang boat goods. Outbound traffic from this street is constant, leading to tight pricing. Luyang pointed rice is scarce and in demand, so it is similar to the original market. The appetite for Bianyin Yuan is still acceptable, and the trend is hardening. Foreign rice merchants are procuring, but only taking a small amount from the Yangtze River area. The rest of the ports and this street see clear skies, and transactions have become sluggish. Market prices are hovering.

Flour Market Continues to Decline

▲Especially Distant Months

Yesterday, the flour market already showed signs of weakness. Because the weather has cleared up, it is expected that the water will recede everywhere, and the panicked state of outsiders has eased slightly. Manufacturers are still insisting on near-term contracts, but distant contracts continue to be sold off. Generally, people are aware that foreign wheat can continue to be priced, which is an extremely large obstacle to the future. As a result, the market sentiment has weakened. Actual sales of distant contracts are stagnant, and near-term contracts have slightly increased. As a result, the current month fell by 1 fen compared to the previous day, August fell by 2 fen, September and October fell by 1 fen and 7 li and 5 hao, November fell by 1 fen and 5 hao, and December fell by 1 fen.

Wheat Prices Rise Again

▲Yangtze River Customers Fight to Speak

Yesterday, the wheat market was initially flat and then showed a rising trend. Initially, foreign wheat quotations fluctuated by 1 or 2 jiao, and the weather also cleared up, so market sentiment naturally became quiet. However, customers from the Yangtze River area are suffering from severe floods, and grain prices are rising daily, so they are still competing to purchase, causing near and distant months to rise again. As a result, August rose by 5 fen compared to the previous day, September rose by 6 fen, and October to December each rose by 5 fen. Due to standards and rice prices, high-quality current wheat is also being bid up by 1 or 2 fen. Approximately 3,000 bags of wheat from Danyang, Dongtai, Penglai, Dacang, Shuangfeng, Baoshan, Wuxi, and Zhenjiang were purchased by Fuxin Hua and Xinda.

Silk and Tea: Green Tea Transactions Are Unusually Strong

▲Chouxin Zhenmei Top Plate Opens at 270-280 Taels

Yesterday, the local foreign merchant tea market, including green tea from various routes such as Luzhuang, Tuzhuang, and Pingshui, saw unusually strong transactions. Among them, items such as Zhenmei and Xiumei saw market prices rise sharply by 4 or 5 taels. Chouxin Zhenmei top plates have already opened at 270 taels. Tongfu, Jinlong, and other firms are also more actively interested in ordinary Zhenmei from Tunxi, Shexian, Suian, and other routes. However, the selling prices are all low. Low-grade goods from Yushan and Wenzhou have almost sold out. Chinese tea merchants are adopting a firm stance in light of the reduced harvests from various routes this year.

Lyon Japanese Silk Sales Still Strong

The Lyon market has seen sluggish silk sales since the beginning of summer. Although the silk weaving factories are in the summer holiday shutdown period, Japanese silk sales are still strong, and prices are weakening further. Chinese silk is greatly affected. Grade A Japanese silk is only opening at 163 francs per kilogram, Grade B at 125 francs, and Grade C at 92 francs, each falling by 4 or 5 francs.

European and American Silk Sales Are Quiet and Lifeless

Overseas silk factories are shut down for summer vacation, and yellow and white factories are unasked for. Silk telegrams are not being forwarded. Yesterday, only Zhonghe et al. imported 20 bales of white Qianjing silk, and Kechang imported 15 bales of yellow coarse silk. Prices are all firm.

Sugar Market: 300 Tons of Abandoned Dutch Brown Sugar Traded

▲Ice Flower Green Opens with a Smart Appearance

Yesterday, according to telegrams from the sugar-producing regions, Cuban spot sugar prices were unchanged. New York sugar futures for March were unchanged, May fell by 2 points, and other months each fell by 1 point. Java spot and futures sugar still lacked increases and decreases. Public association clearing buying interest was still quiet. Dutch sugar No. 24 raw white sugar was still at 11 taels and 5 qian, Hong Kong goods were at 11 taels and 4 qian, and No. 20 medium white sugar was at 10 taels and 9 qian and 5 fen. Transactions were sparse, and market conditions were flat. Taikoo granulated sugar spot B mark was clearing at 12 taels, and old goods CW mark were at 11 taels and 8 qian. The trend was also weak. In terms of abandoned goods, Huaxinhao sold 200 tons of Dutch No. 8 raw sugar for shipment in September at a price of 4 yuan, 9 jiao, and 7.5 fen in Dutch currency. The firm's purchasing interest was active. The company's Ice Flower Green is still selling well, so it continues to be offered at a price of 10 taels and 2 qian and 5 fen. Original goods are asking for 10 taels and 4 qian, and market conditions are smart.

North and South Goods: Honey Dates Are Out of Stock

Because those who traded in honey dates suffered huge losses in the previous year, the output was reduced last year, resulting in supply not meeting demand. Market prices are gradually rising. When the inventory was lacking, "秃秃" were sold for as much as 37 or 38 taels, and finally reached 42 taels, which was a rare high price. For example, small honey dates from Xinghua were previously only 11 or 12 taels, but this year they are also selling for 30 taels. They are now out of stock and are waiting for new loans to come to the market.

Metals: Overall Market Trend Turns Stable

Metal transactions have been extremely sluggish due to the continuous heavy rain. Yesterday, the weather cleared up, and the market became lively, and the market situation also became stable. There were transactions in British and American goods, tinplate, and over 1,100 boxes were offered. The price of 90-pound British goods increased by 5 fen, selling for 14 taels and 5 qian and 5 fen. Tianjin and Qingdao merchants were competing for 7.5 li patterned British steel plates, with a price of 6 taels and 6 qian. The ordnance factory purchased 700-800 dan of 26-foot and 18-sheet black iron sheets yesterday, with a price of 11 taels and 5 qian. 400-500 dan of No. 16 to No. 20 new lead wire were sold yesterday, with the Sichuan merchants having the strongest purchasing appetite, with a price of 13 taels and 5 qian. The steel bar market was no longer as sluggish as before yesterday, with a price estimated at 91 taels and 5 qian. Although it fell by 1 tael and 5 qian compared to before, the transaction volume was higher than before. The purchasers were all construction merchants. Export business has little hope because all areas are suffering from floods. No. 5 white lead sheets have been slightly more active recently, with a price estimated at 25 taels. Angle iron and new foreign yuan are still stable in the near market. There were only a few transactions in tin and blue lead yesterday, but the supply is not large, and the market is still stable. Because there are still no goods from Hunan Province, the market for pure antimony is good, but in terms of prices, there is no hope of price increases because merchants from Hankou are selling off distant futures.

Market News

▲ Dachang Silk Shop at the intersection of Third Malu and Shilu declares: Our shop has been established for many years and has always been known for its low prices and good quality. Now, because our shop's address needs to be rebuilt, fences have been erected, and the building will be demolished soon. In order to clear a large batch of inventory, our shop has to reluctantly reduce prices for sale, regardless of losses. The discounts on various goods are as low as 70%, which can be described as a grand sale amidst a chorus of low prices. Those who want to purchase cheap clothing materials should not miss this opportunity.

▲ The Meilong Perfume Company on 克利克路 (Keli Ke Road) declares: The Dragon Head brand refined camphor produced by our company has been popular for a long time for its fine quality and low price. It is especially effective for preventing epidemics, dispelling filth, killing insects, and preventing moths. During this hot summer, everyone is preparing and every family is purchasing it. As a result, sales are brisk. In addition, in the recent surge of advocating for domestic goods, we are offering special discounts, which is an excellent opportunity for buyers.

▲ Guanshengyuan declares: Fenghua Maochang Garden has fertile soil and is a famous garden for plant products. The jade dew honey peaches produced there are flavorful and fresh, making them the best in the Zhejiang province. Recently, the peaches have ripened and are being shipped to Shanghai in large quantities, exclusively managed by our company. Recently, our company's Nanjing Road main store, Henan Road branch, 法大馬路 (Fa Da Malu) branch, and old store in the Nine Acres area are all selling them. The price per pound ranges from 35 cents to several tens of cents.

Chen Junming's Seal Engravings

▲ The Lianyi Trading Company next to the Wanguo Cinema on Dongxi Huade Road, Hongkou, declares: The Lianyi stationery, artistically crafted and manufactured by our company, has been extremely popular since its introduction to the market, selling well at home and abroad in large numbers. Among them, such as the Haiyue Jiagong, 科舉 (Keju), Luodi, and others, are highly appreciated by literati and elegant scholars. The Zhongshan stationery and Mingxing stationery are especially popular among students. The newly invented loose-leaf stationery and envelopes are even more popular among the general public, with demand exceeding supply. Other products, such as newly packaged stationery and artistic postcards, are also selling well.

▲ The New Machine Journal Agency at No. 251, Lane 2, Zhejiang Road, declares: In view of the importance of employment opportunities for female students, this agency has specially published a special issue for the twelfth issue to discuss this issue. The content is mostly works by women, which are very insightful and relevant. It also describes the situation of female students serving in various sectors, with unique descriptions that are not easily explained to outsiders. It was published yesterday.

Medical News

The residence of female doctor Chen Jingfang, located at the end of the North Fragrant Powder Lane, Bao'an Alley, East Head of Zhejiang Road, declares: This female doctor has been practicing in Shanghai for more than ten years, specializing in various departments of gynecology and pediatrics, using both acupuncture and medicine, and is rich in experience. She is especially skilled in obstetric surgery and has served as the chief physician in major hospitals in this city, treating countless male and female patients from all over. In order to facilitate patients in the Hongkou area, a branch clinic has been established in the Sino-French Pharmacy at the Zhonghongqiao pier on Dongxi Huade Road. The time is from 2 pm to 4 pm every day, closed on Sundays, and at other times at the epidemic hospital of the Chinese Red Cross Society, west of the New World.

▲ In today's newspaper's theater program column, there is an advertisement offering a reward of 200 gold coins for the capture of the masked girl. This reward is offered by the Ming Garden. It is said that anyone who provides information leading to the arrest, or who captures her on the spot, will be rewarded in full. According to reports, the girl is the mastermind behind the destruction of the Far East Happy Seed. She obtained the Happy Seed and spread it in the Ming Garden. The girl's name is Miss Taylor. A photograph of her is attached above. Tomorrow, Xu Guo, the chief detective of Ming Garden, will announce the news of the arrest.

Page 21

Youth Corner

Beside the Volcano

— Sha Qing

About a month ago, I was still besieged by poverty and illness beside a volcano in a foreign country. That volcano had undergone several violent activities, and I almost got buried under the volcano. According to the measurements of geologists and volcano experts, that volcano was in the midst of an eruption because it was a sleeping volcano, just like people who fall asleep at night must wake up in the morning. It had been sleeping for a long time.

It had been sleeping for forty-five years. When it was awake forty-five years ago, it was said that tens of thousands of lives were completely swallowed by it. Now, there are still some remnants left on the foothills by the sea. The huge seaships, machine wheels, steam boilers, steam cabinets, and smokestacks that were destroyed by the sea are scattered haphazardly on the foothills and covered with red rust and green mold. No matter who sees that kind of heartbreaking and tragic wreckage, they would probably not dare to recall the scene at that time.

A school beside the volcano seemed like an unfortunate death trap because not long after I arrived there, I was entangled by illness. My body gradually became as thin as a ghost. However, due to the pressure of life and the cost of medical treatment, I had to support my weak and sickly body and run to the classroom to struggle desperately. After the whole day's work was finished, the mountain of test papers piled up on the desk completely absorbed my spirit and brainpower. From that time on, I was sick and unable to get out of bed.

A small dormitory was tightly covered by the deep green shadows of coconut trees. The inside was eerily quiet. At that time, I didn't seem to feel any sadness, just drowsily sleeping on the bed, quietly listening to my own heartstrings beating, and staring blankly at the electric light hanging by the window. Every time the electric light swayed very violently, I knew there was an earthquake. In normal times, I always felt that earthquakes were very scary, but when I was sick, this thought was completely reversed.

One day, a little after 1 am, the people in the entire village and town at the foot of the mountain were all immersed in their dreams. Suddenly, a heart-wrenching siren sounded outside. I opened my sleepy eyes and saw the electric light swaying back and forth non-stop, turning into a cradle for a loving mother. At that time, I was also as weak as a baby lying on the bed, unable to get up.

The next morning, a friend came to visit and told me about the signs of the volcano erupting three months ago. It was at noon one day when the earth's crust shook violently, and a sound echoed faintly from underground. Evil smoke filled the mountains, and the sky was dark and lightless. Many people were carrying flashlights and running towards the neighboring mountain peaks, like a tragic scene that had been shown in a movie.

I was bitterly entangled by illness there for more than two months, and it was only with great effort that I managed to break free. Now, I have finally left that dangerous volcano and safely returned to my homeland.

I was after all, stunned

— Jun Shan

This is a very special ending ah. My four years of university life, here, is declared its final ending.

The registrar's announcement has already been posted, saying that our class will stop classes from tomorrow. The two words "stop classes", in the past, how much would they stir people's heartstrings. Although it is said that in our school, attending or not attending classes is entirely up to our own happiness to decide. If you are not willing, then absenting yourself from a few days of class without any reason will not cause any problems. But today's news of the cessation of classes has brought us an indescribable sense of sadness, contrary to expectations. The dormitory, which was usually full of joyful laughter, now has an added layer of dismal fog. Everyone seemed to be silent, as if they had been struck dumb. Happy smiles had also quietly slipped away from everyone's face. Oh, we all felt that the time of the past four years will never again be revealed on our future journey through life. Although the life of these past four years has been so ordinary, monotonous and boring, at this moment when we are about to shake hands with it for the last time, we finally feel that this is also a meaningful and valuable process that is worth our consideration. Yes, in these past four years, it has been very kindly giving us a lot of precious gifts, but, these gifts oh, we have all inadvertently put aside. Really, in our group, how many people have not failed its kindness.

Now, this is our last lesson. Mr. Xie, who has the best relationship with us, walked onto the podium with a briefcase, his face full of sorrow, dragging his legs that seemed very tired, but she didn't, as an exception, call out the names, nor did she open the book, but just stared at us. Naturally, we were the same, not making a sound.

"Oh, this is your last lesson," Mr. Xie finally spoke, but even in our class, which was usually known for its mischievousness, finally no one dared to come out and say "Yes" in response, but rather made the air, which was already very silent, even more oppressive. It became even more deathly silent.

"At this time, are you feeling any emotion inside?"

"Okay, let's not talk about these anymore. We're about to say goodbye. We should each say more comforting words to bless each other," Mr. Xie's nose seemed to be a little sore too, but the so-called comforting words only appeared in each of our minds, and then quickly disappeared like bubbles. We spent a very sacred forty minutes like this, and our last lesson was, after all, driven away by the relentless fire wheel of the god of time, never to return. How can we not be attached? We deeply regret it. Knowing that time is so easy to pass, why have we always been so casual?

"Okay, goodbye, everyone. Fortunately, we are all still young. Even if we say goodbye, we will never lack the opportunity to reunite in society in the future. Work hard, strive, cherish, everyone," Mr. Xie quickly finished these words and disappeared like a startled goose in our eyes. At the same time, I also thought of a sentence from Jiang Yan's Hate Fu, "Those who are sadly despondent are those who are leaving." In a week's time, wouldn't our group be flying apart like swallows, each going their own way? How can the reunions of the past be expected in the future, and isn't it the case that, except for one or two lucky ones, we are all blindly heading towards that dark and united society, searching for each person's destination? Oh, who can guarantee that no one is in danger, and that we can repeat that past life that, although was ordinary and boring, was still very peaceful?

Oh, I was, after all, stunned.

Youth Corner Submission Guidelines

(1) Articles should focus on discussions about youth issues, news about domestic and foreign schools or students, essays, descriptions of school life, essays, etc., and the style is not limited.

(2) Books are limited to those dealing with youth issues.

(3) Photos related to youth life (such as sports, travel, sightseeing, drama performances, lectures, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements are acceptable. Whether individual or group, all are welcome. Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(4) The number of words in each article should not exceed 2,000.

(5) Write horizontally, do not write sloppily, and omit Western words where possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

Regardless of whether the submitted manuscripts are published or not, they will not be returned. If a return is required,

(6) Do not write horizontally in the manuscript, do not write sloppily, omit Western words where possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation

(7) Do not use blue ink to draw pictures, and do not use colored paper. Use , black ink to draw.

(8) Please indicate that the submission should be sent to the Youth Corner Editorial Department.
